[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m139[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m140[0m[39m:    ret->mem = [0m[1;35mxmlMalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mret->size + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m141[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mret->mem == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m142[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mret[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Issue Analysis & Root Cause[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The heap‐buffer‐overflow is triggered in encoding.c’s UTF32ToUTF8 function, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically in the single‐byte branch:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc < [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         in += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         out += [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Unlike the multi‐byte branches, this path lacks a boundary check against [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`outend`, so when `out == outend` it writes one byte past the allocated region [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39minto the redzone[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, causing the overflow.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The buffer was allocated with `size + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` bytes in xmlBufCreate [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfor a null [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mterminator[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but xmlBufAvail exposes only `size` bytes of usable space. The missing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck leads to overwriting the redzone.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical Constraints[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preserve existing UTF-[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m→UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m conversion logic, including how multi‐byte [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msequences handle buffer fullness.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not alter fuzzing harness or tests.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not change buffer allocation policies in buf.c beyond necessary checks.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintain compatibility with xmlBuf API expectations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e., buffer has an extra[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbyte reserved for termination[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Outline[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In encoding.c, within UTF32ToUTF8 near the c<[0m[1;36m0x80[0m[39m case, insert a guard [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentical in spirit to the UTF16→UTF32 loop’s boundary check.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Specifically, before writing `out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c;`, verify that at least one byte of [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutput space remains:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc < [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Prevent single‐byte overflow: require [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte available *[0m[35m/[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout >= outend[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             break;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         in += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         out += [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This mirrors the pattern in lines [0m[1;36m2809[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m2813[0m[39m:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc < [0m[1;36m0x10000[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout >= outend[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             break;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c & [0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c >> [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         …[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other branches or code paths require adjustment—multi‐byte branches already[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out < n[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break`.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `encoding.c` and locate the `UTF32ToUTF8` function around line [0m[1;36m2867[0m[39m.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Directly above the assignment `out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c;` in the `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc < [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minsert:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout >= outend[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          break;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Recompile and run the existing test suite [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding fuzz harness[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to ensure:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - No buffer overflows occur in AddressSanitizer builds.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - All functional tests and fuzz tests pass [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e., no unintended truncation in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormal use[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Review any callsites relying on the exact number of output bytes; adjust [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdocumentation if necessary to note that output may be truncated if target buffer is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfull.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification & Side‐Effects[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This minimal guard directly addresses the one‐byte overflow without altering [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother logic.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It preserves how multi‐byte sequences behave under buffer pressure.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - On buffer exhaustion, UTF32ToUTF8 will now exit the conversion loop gracefully[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrather than corrupt memory. Consumers of the API receive a truncated output but [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbenefit from safety.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar boundary checks exist elsewhere in encoding.c [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., UTF16 loops[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis change aligns UTF32 handling with the established pattern.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Potential side‐effect: truncated output on exact‐boundary conditions. [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMitigation: callers should check return values or buffer fullness if full [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mround‐trip of content is required.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. No Harness or Test Code Changes[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzz harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzz/html.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and any XML tests remain untouched.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures existing test coverage continues to operate unchanged, with the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madded benefit of avoiding sanitizer failures.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2909[0m[39m:            out += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2910[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2911[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2912[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2913[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39min-instart > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2915[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2918[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mret[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2919[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mencoding.[0m[1;92mc:2743[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2765[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2743[0m[39m:    const unsigned char *inend;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2744[0m[39m:    unsigned char *outstart = out;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2745[0m[39m:    unsigned char *outend;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2746[0m[39m:    unsigned c, d;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2747[0m[39m:    int ret = XML_ENC_ERR_SPACE;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2748[0m[39m:    int i, len;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2749[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* UTF32 encoding has no BOM *[0m[35m/[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2750[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mout == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutlen == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39minlen == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2751[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXML_ENC_ERR_INTERNAL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2752[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39min == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2753[0m[39m:   [0m[39m*outlen = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2754[0m[39m:   [0m[39m*inlen = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2755[0m[39m:   [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2756[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2757[0m[39m:    inend = in + *inlen;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2758[0m[39m:    outend = out + [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*outlen & ~[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2759[0m[39m:    while [0m[1;39m([0m[39min < inend[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2760[0m[39m:        c = in[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2761[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2762[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc < [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2763[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout >= outend[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2764[0m[39m:                break;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2765[0m[39m:            out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Introduce an output-end pointer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`outend`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in `UTF32ToUTF8` to represent the end[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof the output buffer.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. After the existing declaration of `outstart`, add:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      unsigned char *outend = out + *outlen;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      This uses the initial `*outlen` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe capacity of the output buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompute the valid write boundary.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Before each multi-branch write in the conversion loop, guard against writes that[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwould exceed `outend`. Concretely, modify the loop starting at line ~[0m[1;36m2857[0m[39m so that [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meach branch checks if there is sufficient space:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For the [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte sequence [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`c < [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, ensure at least [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte remains:[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out < [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For the [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte sequence [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`c < [0m[1;36m0x800[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, ensure at least [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m bytes remain:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out < [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For the [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-byte sequence [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m([0m[39mc & [0m[1;36m0xF800[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0xD800[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, ensure at least [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m bytes [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out < [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For the [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte surrogate-fallback sequence, ensure at least [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes remain:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out < [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Remove any previous ad hoc references to an undeclared `outend` variable. The [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnew `outend` declaration provides the correct scope and definition.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preserve existing logic:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The break on insufficient space causes the loop to exit and fall through to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe final length updates.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The return value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ret`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m logic remains intact: on partial or full conversion, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ret` is set to the number of bytes written.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. No other parts of the codebase, fuzz harness, or tests are modified. This patch [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monly changes `UTF32ToUTF8` in `encoding.c`, preserving all existing functionality [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand test coverage.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Defining `outend` prevents undefined compilation errors while giving a canonical [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundary pointer.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Branch-specific checks mirror the established pattern in `UTF8ToUTF32`, ensuring [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno writes past the buffer.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Break-based early exit cleanly propagates converted-byte counts without altering [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe established `ret` handling.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This approach fully addresses the [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand any future multi-byte [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflows[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m by systematically preventing out-of-bounds writes.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Side Effects: minimal. Conversion stops when space is exhausted. Clients receive [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpartial conversions encoded safely. Existing API semantics and error codes [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`XML_ENC_ERR_SPACE`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are preserved.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Similar pattern: see `UTF8ToUTF32` in `encoding.c` around lines [0m[1;36m2743[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m2765[0m[39m, which [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muses an `outend` guard for [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte writes. We replicate that idiom for the reverse [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconversion.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
